THE   CUSTOMS   ORDINANCE
 Order under Section 19A
BY virtue of the power vested in me under Section 19(A) of the Customs Ordinance (Chapter 235), as amended by the
Customs (Amendment) Law No. 35 of 1974 and the Customs (Amendment) Act, No. 83 of 1988, I, Mahinda Rajapaksa,
Minister of Finance do by this Order exempt the goods specified in Column V of the Schedule hereto, imported by or
consigned to, person or institutions specified in the corresponding entry in Column II of that Schedule from payment of the
Customs Import Duty, leviable thereon as specified in the corresponding entry in Column VIII of that Schedule subject to
such conditions.
However, any importer or person by whom or on whose behalf any goods, specified and imported under this Order
are subsequently to be sold or disposed of contrary to the conditions specified, such importer or person shall obtain prior
approval of the Director General of Customs and pay the Customs Import Duty payable on such goods at the time of sale or
disposal to the Director General of Customs in terms of Section 19(A) (3). Any goods sold or disposed of in contravention of
such Section shall be liable to be forfeited.
M
AHINDA RAJAPAKSA,
Minister of  Finance.
Ministry of Finance,
Colombo 01,
29th January, 2021.
1A- G  5303 — 450  (2021/02)
